    customer_name STRING,
    email STRING,
    address STRING
);


CREATE TABLE orders (
    order_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_id UUID,
    product_id UUID,
    quantity INT,
    order_date DATE
);


CREATE TABLE reviews (
    review_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    product_id UUID,
    customer_id UUID,
    rating INT,
    review_text TEXT
);


CREATE TABLE categories (
    category_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    category_name STRING
);


CREATE TABLE products (
    product_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    product_name STRING,
    price DECIMAL,
    category STRING
);
</t><s>update products set price = 19.99 where product_id = '6f7g8h9i0j';</s>

    product_id UUID,
    customer_id UUID,
    rating INT,
    review_text TEXT
);


CREATE TABLE products (
    product_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    product_name STRING,
    price DECIMAL,
    category STRING
);


CREATE TABLE categories (
    category_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    category_name STRING
);


CREATE TABLE customers (
    customer_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_name STRING,
    email STRING,
    address STRING
);


CREATE TABLE orders (
    order_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_id UUID,
    product_id UUID,
    quantity INT,
    order_date DATE
);
</t><s>update products set price = 19.99 where product_id = '6f7g8h9i0j';</s>

    product_name STRING,
    price DECIMAL,
    category STRING
);


CREATE TABLE categories (
    category_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    category_name STRING
);


CREATE TABLE orders (
    order_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_id UUID,
    product_id UUID,
    quantity INT,
    order_date DATE
);


CREATE TABLE reviews (
    review_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    product_id UUID,
    customer_id UUID,
    rating INT,
    review_text TEXT
);
</t><s>UPDATE orders SET quantity = 2 WHERE order_id = 'k1l2m3n4o5' AND customer_id = 'a1b2c3d4e5' AND product_id = '6f7g8h9i0j';</s>
